We also use this information to measure how users respond to our marketing efforts. For example, we use information collected to investigate suspicious activity or violations of our terms or policies, detect when someone needs help, and protect our or others’ rights or property.</p></li></ul><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz"><span class="x117nqv4">3. How is information shared?</span></div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Our Meta VR Products help you engage with the XR ecosystem and others that interact with it. To provide and support our Meta VR Products, information we have about you is shared in certain circumstances. Here is who can see information about you when you and others use our Meta VR Products.</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">People and accounts you share and communicate with on our Meta VR Products.</span> When you share, interact, and communicate using our Meta VR Products, you choose the audience for what you share. For example, when you share a photo or other content in a shared or public virtual space, other people who visit the space may be able to see it.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Public Information.</span> Certain information you post to your Meta Quest profile, such as your Meta Quest ID (also known as your Meta Quest Username), and avatar, will be public and visible to people on and off our Meta VR Products. Your Meta Quest ID is a unique identifier you choose to identify yourself on our Meta VR Products.<br>Information you post to public areas of our Meta VR Products, such as a forum, blog, or other community tool, will also be visible to people on and off our Meta VR Products. If you post information to these interactive features, it will be publicly available. Certain information associated with your public posts, such as the time of your post, also will be published and publicly available.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Content others share about you.</span> You should consider who you choose to share with, because people who are able to see your activity, content, or information on our Meta VR Products may choose to share it with others on and off our Meta VR Products. For example, when you interact with others in a multiplayer game, another player could choose to livestream that experience – including what you are doing in the game – to Meta. People may also use Meta VR Products to share content about you they have obtained from other sources.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Apps, Developers, and Other Online Content Providers on our Meta VR Products.</span> You can interact with third-party content, games, apps, and other experiences through our Meta VR Products. We share information about you with these partners so they can provide you with the experiences you've requested, such as:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Information in your Meta Quest profile and about how you use our Meta VR Products. For example, we make available to third party developers a list of your friends who also use the developer’s app so they can offer to pair you in a game or other experience within their app, or rank your scores and achievements in that app against your friends’ scores and achievements.  We also share information about individual abuse reports or abuse statistics on our Meta VR Products, so we can help develop a safe and enjoyable XR ecosystem.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Information about your interaction with the third-party service, such as how long you have interacted with content.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Any other information you choose to share with the third party.</p></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Third-party content providers may also collect information from you directly through the experiences they provide. Please note that any information you share with these (or other) third parties will be subject to those third parties’ own privacy policies, not this one.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Sharing Within Related Companies.</span> We share information with related companies, including the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/help/111814505650678" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Companies</a>, depending on which services you use, including to promote safety, integrity and security across the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/help/195227921252400" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Company Products</a>. For example, if you buy something on or through the Meta VR Products, we share your information with Meta Platforms Technologies, LLC to process your payment and detect, prevent, or otherwise address fraud, security, or technical issues in accordance with the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="/legal/quest/store-terms-of-sale/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_self">Meta Quest Store Terms</a>. We also share information with Meta Platforms Technologies, LLC and Meta Platforms Technologies Ireland Ltd. to conduct and support research and innovation to further the state of the art or academic understanding of XR technology.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Service providers.</span> We share the information we collect with vendors, service providers, researchers and other partners, who work at our direction to support the Meta VR Products (such as hosting our Meta VR Products, fulfilling orders, facilitating payments, analyzing the way people use our Meta VR Products, processing credit card payments, providing customer service, or sending electronic communications for us). For example, we share recordings and transcripts of your voice interactions with vendors and service providers who assist us in improving, troubleshooting, and training our speech recognition systems.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Other parties in connection with certain business transactions.</span> In the event that the ownership of Meta (or any portion of our assets) changes as a result of a merger, acquisition, or in the event of a bankruptcy, information from or about you or your device will be transferred to another company.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Permission.</span> We share your information for any other purpose you choose.</p></li><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl"><span class="x117nqv4">Law enforcement or legal requests.</span> We share information with law enforcement or in response to legal requests in the circumstances outlined in Section 7 below.</p></li></ul><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We also share de-identified or aggregate data with others. De-identified data means information where we have removed your name and other data that could reasonably be used to identify you. Aggregate data is data that has been combined with other data so that it doesn’t identify any specific person. For example, we provide developers with aggregated statistics about the number of people from a particular region that use our Meta VR Products, so developers can create content tailored for people in that market</p><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz"><span class="x117nqv4">4. How Oculus Works with the Rest of Meta</span></div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We share infrastructure, systems and technology with the rest of <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/help/111814505650678" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta</a> (which includes Instagram and WhatsApp) to provide an innovative, relevant, consistent and safe experience across all <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://www.facebook.com/help/1561485474074139" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Meta Products</a> you use. We also process information about you across Meta for these purposes, as permitted by applicable law and in accordance with their terms and policies. For example, we use information about bad actors on Meta Quest to fight spam or abuse on other Meta Products like Instagram. We also work to understand how people use and interact with Meta Products, like understanding the number of unique users on different Meta Products.</p><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz"><span class="x117nqv4">5. Third Parties that Provide Content, Marketing, or Functionality on Our Services</span></div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Some of the content, marketing, and functionality on our Meta VR Products is provided by third parties that are not affiliated with us. For example, we work with companies that help us understand how people use our Meta VR Products.</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">Other companies may collect information on or through our Meta VR Products to market to you on or off of our Meta VR Products. These and other third parties may collect information about your use of our Meta VR Products, including through the use of cookies, device IDs, local storage, pixels and other technologies, and this information may be collected over time and combined with information collected on different websites and online services.</p><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz"><span class="x117nqv4">6. Data retention and deletion</span></div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We store Meta Quest data that identifies you until it is no longer necessary to provide our Meta VR Products or your Oculus account is deleted, whichever comes first, unless retention of the data for a longer period is justified in order to comply with law or recordkeeping obligations, to respond to a legal request, prevent harm, or to improve our safety, integrity and security features. This is a case-by-case determination that depends on things like the nature of the data, why it is collected and processed, and relevant legal, integrity or operational retention needs. For example, we retain certain purchase information for accounting and tax purposes even after you have deleted your account.</p><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">When you delete your account, we delete things you have posted and information about apps and entitlements you have downloaded, and you will not be able to recover that information later. Information that others have shared about you is not part of your account and will not be deleted when you delete your account. To delete your account at any time, or to learn more about deleting your account, please visit the <a class="x1i10hfl x1qjc9v5 xjbqb8w xjqpnuy xa49m3k xqeqjp1 x2hbi6w x13fuv20 xu3j5b3 x1q0q8m5 x26u7qi x972fbf xcfux6l x1qhh985 xm0m39n x9f619 x1ypdohk xdl72j9 xdt5ytf x2lah0s xe8uvvx xdj266r x11i5rnm xat24cr x1mh8g0r x2lwn1j xeuugli xexx8yu x4uap5 x18d9i69 xkhd6sd x16tdsg8 xggy1nq x1ja2u2z x1t137rt xt0psk2 x1bvjpef xt0b8zv xmy21w2 x1uhb9sk" href="https://secure.oculus.com/my/privacy/" role="link" tabindex="0" target="_blank">Privacy Center</a>.</p><div class="x16g9bbj x1p5oq8j xwxc41k xfjrbgk xw8udss xobpncf xjliv6m x1ij0wma xsp84uj x1uc5f31 xxgyeuj x166pohu xu0txxm xcxolhg xwczod1 x13mtej6 xjlskvi x1kanymm x1i6xp69 xr4g9wi x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl x1a2a7pz"><span class="x117nqv4">7. How do we respond to legal requests and prevent harm?</span></div><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">We access, preserve and share information with regulators, law enforcement or others:</p><ul class="x1xfsgkm xtaz4m5"><li class="x8dyrlr x1jchvi3 xo1l8bm xjat59b x1evy7pa"><p class="x16g9bbj xdj266r xat24cr xwxc41k xw8udss x17gzxuv x3a6nna xm5vtmc x1t2x7uc x1o1n6r0 x1wsgf3v x1c773n9 x1k03ns3 xpbi8i2 x9820fh x1npfmwo xhj0du5 xrm2kyc xjprkx4 xlu1awn x12429cg x6tc29j xbq7h4v x6jdkww xq9mrsl">In response to a legal request (like a search warrant, court order or subpoena), if we have a good faith belief that the law requires us to do so.
